<HTML><HEAD>
<TITLE>EX-99.1</TITLE>
</HEAD>
 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt" ALIGN="center">


<IMG SRC="g256519g08a65.jpg" ALT="LOGO">
 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Arcellx Provides Business Highlights and Reports Second Quarter 2022 Financial Results </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>&#151; </B>Completed upsized <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">follow-on</FONT> offering of common stock, raising $128.8&nbsp;million in
gross proceeds including full exercise of underwriters&#146; option to purchase additional shares &#151; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">&#151; Presented continued robust
long-term responses from its CART-ddBCMA Phase 1 expansion trial being evaluated in patients with r/r MM at the 2022 ASCO Annual Meeting &#151; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">&#151; Preclinical results from CART-ddBCMA published in <I><U>Molecular Cancer Therapeutics</U> </I>&#151; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">REDWOOD CITY, Calif., Aug.&nbsp;15, 2022 /PRNewswire/ &#151; Arcellx, Inc. (NASDAQ: ACLX), a biotechnology company reimagining cell therapy through the
development of innovative immunotherapies for patients with cancer and other incurable diseases, today reported business highlights and financial results for the second quarter ended June&nbsp;30, 2022. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;We are excited about the rapid progress we&#146;ve made since becoming a public company in February of this year,&#148; said Rami Elghandour,
Arcellx&#146;s <U>Chairman and Chief Executive Officer</U>. &#147;In the second quarter, we achieved meaningful milestones with the presentation of new clinical data for our lead product candidate, CART-ddBCMA, during an oral presentation at ASCO;
strengthened our balance sheet with a successful <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">follow-on</FONT> offering, raising gross proceeds of $128.8&nbsp;million; dosed our first patient in <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">ACLX-001,</FONT> our Phase 1
study utilizing our Arc-SparX technology; and expanded our management team and Board of Directors with exceptional professionals adding to the diversity of our team. In the second half of this year, we look forward to presenting an encore
presentation of our CART-ddBCMA Phase 1 study at ESMO, initiating our Phase 2 pivotal CART-ddBCMA (iMMagine) trial in patients with relapsed or refractory multiple myeloma (r/r MM), presenting longer-term patient data from our Phase 1 CART-ddBCMA
expansion trial in r/r MM, and initiating our Phase 1 ARC-SparX clinical trial of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">ACLX-002</FONT> in patients with acute myeloid leukemia and high-risk myelodysplastic syndrome. We&#146;re committed to
establishing&nbsp;Arcellx&nbsp;as a leading cell therapy&nbsp;organization&nbsp;by&nbsp;continuing&nbsp;to scale our business,&nbsp;advancing our novel&nbsp;platform&nbsp;to&nbsp;help as many patients as possible, and&nbsp;attracting and
retaining&nbsp;exceptional talent.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Recent Business Highlights </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Completed upsized public offering of common stock and underwriters&#146; full exercise of option to purchase additional shares. </B>On June&nbsp;21, 2022,
Arcellx announced the closing of its upsized public offering of 8,050,000 shares of common stock, which included the full exercise by the underwriters of their option to purchase an additional 1,050,000 shares of common stock, at a price to the
public of $16.00 per share. The aggregate gross proceeds raised in the offering were $128.8&nbsp;million, before deducting underwriting discounts and commissions and offering expenses, payable by Arcellx. All shares in the offering were offered by
Arcellx. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Appointed Maryam Abdul-Kareem as General Counsel. </B>On June&nbsp;21, 2022, Arcellx appointed Maryam
Abdul-Kareem as General Counsel. Ms.&nbsp;Abdul-Kareem brings extensive legal and business expertise in the biopharmaceutical industry, including serving in senior positions at Kinnate Biopharma and AstraZeneca. At Arcellx, she will oversee a broad
spectrum of legal, contracts, and compliance matters.</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Presented continued robust long-term responses from lead product candidate, CART-ddBCMA, being
evaluated in a Phase 1 expansion trial in patients with relapsed or refractory multiple myeloma at the 2022 ASCO Annual Meeting. </B>On June&nbsp;3, 2022, Arcellx presented new clinical data from its ongoing Phase 1 expansion study of its novel,
autologous, CART-ddBCMA therapy for the treatment of patients with r/r MM during an oral presentation at the 2022 American Society of Clinical Oncology Annual Meeting. The data demonstrated 100% ORR; deep and durable responses were observed in
patients with poor prognostic factors. Overall, 22 of 31 (71%) evaluable patients reached CR/sCR. Of the 16 patients who have had their <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">12-month</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">follow-up</FONT> visit,
including 8 patients (50%) who have EMD, 13 (81%) have reached CR/sCR with 9 patients (56%) remaining in ongoing response with a median follow up of 17.7 months. No cases of Grade &#8805;3 CRS and no delayed neurotoxicity or parkinsonian-like events
were observed at the recommended Phase 2 dose of 100&nbsp;million CAR+ cells (n=25). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Preclinical results from CART-ddBCMA published in
</B><B><I>Molecular Cancer Therapeutics</I></B><B>.</B> In June 2022, Arcellx&#146;s preclinical results for its CART-ddBCMA candidate were published in <I>Molecular Cancer Therapeutics</I> in an article entitled,<I> &#147;Preclinical efficacy of
BCMA-directed CAR T cells incorporating a novel D Domain antigen recognition domain.&#148;</I> This report demonstrated that ddBCMA CAR T cells cocultured with BCMA-positive cell lines showed highly potent, dose-dependent<I> in vitro</I> measures of
cytotoxicity, cytokine production, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-cell</FONT> degranulation, and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-cell</FONT> proliferation as well as <I>in vivo</I> tumor suppression in three disseminated BCMA-expressing tumor
models. The full online publication can be accessed <U>here</U>. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Appointed Michelle Gilson as Chief Financial Officer.</B> On May&nbsp;23, 2022,
Arcellx announced the appointment of Michelle Gilson as Chief Financial Officer. Ms.&nbsp;Gilson joins Arcellx from Canaccord Genuity, where most recently she served as Managing Director and Senior Equity Research Analyst covering biotechnology
companies. Ms.&nbsp;Gilson will oversee the company&#146;s finance function and will play a key role in overall corporate strategy. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Expanded Board of
Directors with the appointment of Olivia Ware. </B>On May&nbsp;16, 2022, Arcellx expanded its Board of Directors with the appointment of Olivia Ware. Ms.&nbsp;Ware, a successful executive, brings a wealth of knowledge with more than 20 years of
experience in biotech and pharmaceutical drug development, commercialization, and healthcare management. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Second Quarter 2022 Financial Highlights
</B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Cash, cash equivalents, and marketable securities:</B> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B></B>As of June&nbsp;30, 2022, Arcellx had cash, cash equivalents, and marketable securities of $307.0&nbsp;million, which is anticipated to fund its
operations for at least the next twelve months. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>R&amp;D expenses: </B> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Research and development expenses were $23.4&nbsp;million and $12.6&nbsp;million for the quarters ended June&nbsp;30, 2022 and 2021, respectively, an increase
of $10.8&nbsp;million. This increase was driven by higher external costs associated with the advancement of our CART-ddBCMA clinical program, preclinical development of our other pipeline candidates, and increased headcount. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>G&amp;A expenses:</B> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B></B>General and administrative
expenses were $9.2&nbsp;million and $3.3&nbsp;million for the quarters ended June&nbsp;30, 2022 and 2021, respectively, an increase of $5.9&nbsp;million. This increase was driven by increased headcount, and costs to operate as a public company
during the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2022 as compared to the same period in 2021, including professional fees related to consulting and accounting, audit and legal services. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Net loss: </B> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net loss was $32.1&nbsp;million and
$15.9&nbsp;million for the quarters ended June&nbsp;30, 2022 and 2021, respectively. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About Arcellx, Inc. </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Arcellx, Inc. is a clinical-stage biotechnology company reimagining cell therapy by engineering innovative immunotherapies for patients with cancer and other
incurable diseases. Arcellx believes that cell therapies are one of the forward pillars of medicine and Arcellx&#146;s mission is to advance humanity by developing cell therapies that are safer, more effective, and more broadly accessible.
Arcellx&#146;s lead product candidate, CART-ddBCMA, is being developed for the treatment of relapsed or refractory multiple myeloma (r/r MM) in an ongoing Phase 1 study. CART-ddBCMA has been granted Fast Track, Orphan Drug, and Regenerative Medicine
Advanced Therapy designations by the U.S. Food and Drug Administration. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Arcellx is also advancing its dosable and controllable <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">CAR-T</FONT> therapy, ARC-SparX, through two programs: a Phase 1 study of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">ACLX-001</FONT> for r/r MM, initiated in the second quarter of 2022; and
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">ACLX-002</FONT> in relapsed or refractory acute myeloid leukemia and high-risk myelodysplastic syndrome, expected to enter the clinic in the second half of 2022. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Visit&nbsp;www.arcellx.com&nbsp;for more information. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Forward-looking Statements </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This press release contains
forward-looking statements within the meaning of Section&nbsp;27A of the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, and Section&nbsp;21E of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended. All statements in this press release that are not purely historical
are forward-looking statements, including Arcellx&#146;s expectations regarding the timing and outcomes of clinical trials for its product candidates and publication of related data, the potential impact of its product candidates and platforms on
patients and cell therapy, the timing of achievement of its milestones, its ability to fund operations, and the sufficiency of cash, cash equivalents and marketable securities. The forward-looking statements contained herein are based upon
Arcellx&#146;s current expectations and involve assumptions that may never materialize or may prove to be incorrect. These forward-looking statements are neither promises nor guarantees and are subject to a variety of risks and uncertainties,
including risks that may be found in the section entitled Part II, Item 1A (Risk Factors) in the Quarterly Report on Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">10-Q</FONT> and other documents that Arcellx files from time to time with the Securities and
Exchange Commission. </P>
</DIV></Center>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ARCELLX, INC. </B></P>
